<section class="row">
<div class="col-md-8 col-md-offset-2 text">
<h1>Professor pay-checker</h1>
<p class="byline">By <a href="http://www.dailycal.org/author/schinoy/">SAHIL CHINOY</a> &middot; September 20, 2016</p>
<br>
<p class="lead center">The Daily Californian processed the last decade of payroll information for UC Berkeley faculty, creating the most complete, searchable database of professor and lecturer pay by campus department.</p>
<p class="lead center">We're also releasing the data as part of an <a href="/paychecker/about/#project">open-source effort</a> to make faculty compensation information accessible to the public.</p>
<p class="lead center"><a href="#database">Browse the database</a>, <a href="/paychecker/context/">read context about departmental disparities</a> or <a href="/paychecker/about/">find out more about the data</a>.</p>
</div>
</section>
</div>
</div>
<div class="container">
<section id="database" class="row">
<div class="col-md-10 col-md-offset-1">
<div style="text-align: center">
<h2>Browse the database</h2>
<p><a href="/paychecker/departments/">Compare department averages</a>.<br>
Don't see a professor or lecturer? <a href="/paychecker/about/#caveats">This might be why</a>.</p>
</div>
